<p id="showName" style="font-size:1.5em;">Bulletin of the American Meteorological Society</p>

<script>

let issueURL = window.location.href;

let jrnLoc = issueURL.lastIndexOf("journals");

let startJN = jrnLoc + 9;
let endJN = startJN + 4;

let startVol = endJN + 1;
let endVol = startVol + 2;


let journalName = issueURL.slice(startJN, endJN);
let volume = issueURL.slice(startVol, endVol);

var volumeNumber;

volumeNumber = parseInt(volume);

let journal1 = "bams";
let journal2 = "eint";
let journal3 = "apme";
let journal4 = "atot";
let journal5 = "atsc";
let journal6 = "clim";
let journal7 = "hydr";
let journal8 = "phoc";
let journal9 = "amsm";
let journal10 = "mwre";
let journal11 = "wefo";
let journal12 = "wcas";
let journal13 = "aies";

var name;

if (journalName == journal1) {

name = "Bulletin of the American Meteorological Society";
}
else if (journalName == journal2) {
name = "Earth Interactions";
}

else if ((journalName == journal3) && (volumeNumber >= 1) && (volumeNumber < 22)) {
name = "Journal of Applied Meteorology";
}

else if ((journalName == journal3) && (volumeNumber >= 22) && (volumeNumber < 27)) {
name = "Journal of Climate and Applied Meteorology";
}

else if ((journalName == journal3) && (volumeNumber >= 27) && (volumeNumber < 45)) {
name = "Journal of Applied Meteorology";
}

else if ((journalName == journal3) && (volumeNumber >= 46)) {
name = "Journal of Applied Meteorology and Climatology";
}

else if (journalName == journal4) {
name = "Journal of Atmospheric and Oceanic Technology";
}

else if ((journalName == journal5) && (volumeNumber >= 1) && (volumeNumber < 19)) {
name = "Journal of Meteorology";
}

else if ((journalName == journal5) && (volumeNumber >= 19)) {
name = "Journal of the Atmospheric Sciences";
}

else if (journalName == journal6) {
name = "Journal of Climate";
}

else if (journalName == journal7) {
name = "Journal of Hydrometeorology";
}

else if (journalName == journal8) {
name = "Journal of Physical Oceanography";
}

else if (journalName == journal9) {
name = "Meteorological Monographs";
}

else if (journalName == journal10) {
name = "Monthly Weather Review";
}

else if (journalName == journal11) {
name = "Weather and Forecasting";
}

else if (journalName == journal12) {
name = "Weather, Climate, and Society";
}

else if (journalName == journal13) {

name = "Artificial Intelligence for the Earth Systems";
}

else {

name =" ";
}

document.getElementById("showName").innerHTML = name;

</script>
